library(rjson)
getgoodid = function(t){
  h = fromJSON(t)     #json转化为list
  return(h[[2]][[1]])
}
json1<-as.data.frame(paydata$cartInfo)
json1$`paydata$cartInfo`<-as.character(json1$`paydata$cartInfo`)
newjson1<-apply(table(json1),1,getgoodid())

getgoodid = function(t){

  return(h[[2]][[1]])
}
